         <h3 class="text-mono f4-mktg text-normal color-text-tertiary mb-3"><img alt="GitHub Actions" class="d-inline-block mr-3 position-relative top-1" style="width: 27px;" loading="lazy" src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/modules/site/features/actions-icon-actions.svg">GitHub Actions</h3> 
         <h1 class="h2-mktg mb-3 mx-auto"><span>Automate your workflow</span><br class="actions-hero-text-break"> <span>from</span> <span>idea</span> <span>to</span> <span>production</span></h1> 
         <p class="color-text-tertiary mb-4 mx-auto mx-lg-0" style="max-width: 520px;">GitHub Actions makes it easy to automate all your software workflows, now with world-class CI/CD. Build, test, and deploy your code right from GitHub. Make code reviews, branch management, and issue triaging work the way you want.</p> <a href="https://docs.github.com/actions" class="btn-mktg mb-2">Get started with Actions</a>

       <div class="col-12 col-sm-10 col-md-8 col-lg-6 mx-auto text-center js-build-in-item build-in-scale-fade"> 
        <h2 class="h4-mktg mb-4">Run a workflow<br>on any GitHub event</h2> 
        <p class="f4-mktg color-text-tertiary text-left">Kick off workflows with GitHub events like push, issue creation, or a new release. Combine and configure actions for the services you use, built and maintained by the community.</p> 
        <p class="f4-mktg color-text-tertiary text-left mb-4">Whether you want to build a container, deploy a web service, or automate welcoming new users to your open source projects—there's an action for that. Pair GitHub Packages with Actions to simplify package management, including version updates, fast distribution with our global CDN, and dependency resolution, using your existing GITHUB_TOKEN.</p>

        <div class="col-10 col-lg-5 mx-auto mx-lg-0 pt-8 mb-10 mb-lg-0"> 
         <h2 class="h5-mktg mb-3 text-center text-lg-left">Community-powered workflows</h2> 
         <p class="f4-mktg color-text-tertiary mb-3">GitHub Actions connects all of your tools to automate every step of your development workflow. Easily deploy to any cloud, create tickets in Jira, or publish a package to npm.</p> 
         <p class="f4-mktg color-text-tertiary mb-3">Want to venture off the beaten path? Use the millions of open source libraries available on GitHub to create your own actions. Write them in JavaScript or create a container Action—both can interact with the full GitHub API and any other public API.</p> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <h2 class="h5-mktg mb-7 text-center text-lg-left">What our community is saying</h2> 
       <div class="d-flex gutter gutter-lg-spacious flex-content-stretch flex-wrap mb-8"> 
        <div class="col-12 col-md-6 col-lg-3 mb-7"> 
         <div class="d-flex flex-column"> 
          <div> 
           <img src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/modules/site/features/actions-sonarsource.svg" alt="SonarSource" class="mb-4" loading="lazy"> 
           <blockquote class="color-text-secondary f4 mb-4">
            <span class="float-left ml-n2">“</span>Our mission is to empower all development teams with Code Quality and Security tools. For SonarCloud that means detecting bugs and security vulnerabilities, all while contributing to simple yet powerful pipelines, where multiple tools can play together as a team. GitHub Actions allows just that!”
           </blockquote> 
          </div>

           <blockquote class="color-text-secondary f4 mb-4">
            <span class="float-left ml-n2">“</span>For open source projects, the lower the infrastructure friction we have, the easier it becomes to work with external contributors. Using GitHub Actions for CI and common tasks like triaging issues allows us to lower the barriers even more, so we can focus on writing a good product.”
           </blockquote> 
          </div>

       <div class="position-relative mt-n11 bottom-n11"> 
        <h2 id="pricing-details" class="h5-mktg mb-5 text-center text-lg-left">Simple, pay-as-you-go pricing</h2> 
        <div class="d-flex gutter-spacious flex-items-center flex-wrap flex-lg-nowrap"> 
         <div class="col-10 col-lg-5 mx-auto mx-lg-0 js-build-in"> 
          <div class="bg-blue-dark rounded-2 text-center p-6 position-relative"> 
           <h3 class="h5-mktg color-text-white mt-5">Public repositories</h3> 
           <div class="d-flex flex-items-center flex-justify-center actions-pricing-public"> 
            <div class="text-center position-relative top-n5"> 
             <h3 class="h2-mktg color-text-white">Free</h3>
